)@@G@@@MARVEL     @@@@@@@H@@@@THE @MARVEL PROCESSOR GENERATES CONTROL STATEMENXY
)@@G@@TS TO CALL OTHER PROCESSORS   @G@@@@(@FOR, @MAP, ETC.) TO PROCESS ALL OFXZ
)@@G@@ THE SYMBOLIC ELEMENTS (600 MAX)    @F@@@@ON A PROGRAM FILE.  THE STATEMYA
)@@G@@ENTS GENERATED BY @MARVEL CAN BE    @G@@@@AUTOMATICALLY @ADDED OR THEY CYB
)@@G@@AN BE SAVED IN A SYMBOLIC ELEMENT ON A    @G@@@@PROGRAM FILE.  @MARVEL RYC
)@@G@@EADS DATA CARDS WHICH CAN SUPPLEMENT THE INFOR- @D@@@@MATION GIVEN IN ITYD
)@@G@@S OPTIONS AND SPECIFICATION FIELDS. @@@@@@@D@@@@FORMAT:  @MARVEL[,OPTIONYE
)@@G@@S] [SPEC1.[SPEC2.[SPEC3.]]]   @^@@@@         DIRECTIVE CARDS@B@@@@      YF
)@@G@@   @EOF   <OR NEXT @ CONTROL CARD>  @@@@@@@]@@@@OPTIONS:    @@@@@@@B@@@@YG
)@@G@@  A  PROCESS THE ELEMENTS ALPHABETICALLY  @F@@@@  X  CALL @XREF FOR A CRYH
)@@G@@OSS-REFERENCE LISTING OF ENTRY POINTS AND @#@@@@     REFERENCES.  @C@@@@YI
)@@G@@  S  CALL @SPL TO GENERATE BLOCK LETTER HEADERS @@@@@@@#@@@@SPECIFICATIOYJ
)@@G@@NS:   @@@@@@@G@@@@  SPEC1  THE PROGRAM FILE WHOSE SYMBOLIC ELEMENTS ARE YK
)@@G@@TO BE READ AND    @F@@@@         PROCESSED.  IF SPEC1 IS OMITTED, TPF$ WYL
)@@G@@ILL BE ASSUMED.   @@@@@@@F@@@@  SPEC2  THE PROGRAM FILE ON WHICH THE RELYM
)@@G@@OCATABLE OUTPUT ELEMENTS@F@@@@         (FROM @FOR, @ASM, ETC) AND THE ABYN
)@@G@@SOLUTE OUTPUT ELEMENTS  @G@@@@         (FROM @MAP) ARE TO WRITTEN.  IF SYO
)@@G@@PEC2 IS OMITTED, TPF$ WILL    @#@@@@         BE USED. @@@@@@@G@@@@  SPECYP
)@@G@@3  THE PROGRAM FILE ON WHICH SYMBOLIC OUTPUT ELEMENTS FROM THE    @G@@@@YQ
)@@G@@         PROCESSORS ARE TO BE WRITTEN.  IF SPEC3 IS OMITTED, THERE WILL YR
)@@G@@@B@@@@         BE NO SYMBOLIC OUTPUT ELEMENTS.  @@@@@@@#@@@@DIRECTIVE CAYS
)@@G@@RDS:  @@@@@@@F@@@@ALL DATA CARDS FOR @MARVEL ARE OPTIONAL.  THEY CAUSE @YT
)@@G@@MARVEL TO   @F@@@@CHANGE ITS OUTPUT OR TO GENERATE ADDITIONAL PROCESSOR YU
)@@G@@CALLS.  THEY@A@@@@ARE INDIVIDUALLY DESCRIBED BELOW.   @@@@@@@@@@@@@#@@@@YV
)@@G@@BRK  FILE  ELEMENT@@@@@@@G@@@@THE BRK CARD INHIBITS THE AUTOMATIC @ADDINYW
)@@G@@G OF THE CONTROL STATEMENTS   @F@@@@GENERATED BY @MARVEL AND CAUSES THEMYX
)@@G@@ TO BE WRITTEN ONTO A SYMBOLIC@F@@@@ELEMENT IN A PROGRAM FILE.  THE FILEYY
)@@G@@ NAME MUST APPEAR, WITHOUT A  @F@@@@PERIOD.  THE ELEMENT NAME MAY BE OMIYZ
)@@G@@TTED, IN WHICH CASE, @MARVEL  @G@@@@WILL WRITE THE CONTROL STATEMENTS ONZA
)@@G@@TO AN SDF FILE INSTEAD OF WRITING   @ @@@@THEM ONTO A SYMBOLIC ELEMENT. ZB
)@@G@@@@@@@@@[@@@@SAVE  @@@@@@@G@@@@THE SAVE CARD CAUSES @MARVEL TO WRITE ITS ZC
)@@G@@CONTROL STATEMENTS ONTO A     @G@@@@SYMBOLIC ELEMENT NAMED MARVELCARDS OZD
)@@G@@N THE PROGRAM FILE NAMED IN SPEC3.  @G@@@@SAVE DOES NOT INHIBIT THE @ADDZE
)@@G@@ING OF CONTROL STATEMENTS GENERATED BY    @]@@@@@MARVEL     @@@@@@@[@@@@ZF
)@@G@@PCH   @@@@@@@H@@@@THE PCH CARD CAUSES @MARVEL TO PUNCH THE CONTROL STATEZG
)@@G@@MENTS IT GENERATES.     @@@@@@@^@@@@PROCESSOR   OPTIONS     @@@@@@@H@@@@ZH
)@@G@@THE OPTIONS USED WITH ANY OF THE PROCESSORS CAN BE SPECIFIED BY INCLUDINZI
)@@G@@G     @G@@@@THEM ON A CARD WITH THE PROCESSOR NAME.  IF NO PROCESSOR OPTZJ
)@@G@@IONS ARE    @B@@@@USED, @MARVEL WILL ASSUME THE FOLLOWING:  @@@@@@@[@@@@ZK
)@@G@@FOR  S@[@@@@ASM  S@[@@@@MAP  S@#@@@@PDP  L, FL, OR CL @[@@@@ELT  L@]@@@@ZL
)@@G@@COB  BERS   @[@@@@ALG  S@[@@@@DOC  S@@@@@@@A@@@@PROCESSOR=NEWPROCESSOR  ZM

)@@G@@@[@@@@MER   @@@@@@@F@@@@THE MER CARD CAUSES @DCTNRY TO BE EXECUTED ONLY AA
)@@G@@ONCE, AT THE END  @F@@@@OF ALL THE FORTRAN COMPILATIONS, INSTEAD OF SEPAAB
)@@G@@RATE EXECUTIONS   @F@@@@FOR EACH COMPILATION.  MER IS NECESSARY IF THE MAC
)@@G@@ OPTION IS USED   @#@@@@ON THE DCT CARD.  @@@@@@@^@@@@PUN  OPTIONS,SEQ-CAD
)@@G@@HAR   @@@@@@@F@@@@THE PUN CARD CAUSES ALL OF THE ELEMENTS OF SELECTED TYAE
)@@G@@PES FROM THE@G@@@@FILE NAMED IN SPEC1 OF THE @MARVEL STATEMENT TO BE PUNAF
)@@G@@CHED.  OPTIONS    @F@@@@FOR THE PUN CARD INCLUDE N, S, R, A, G, J, AND HAG
)@@G@@.  THE N OPTION   @G@@@@INHIBITS ALL OTHER FUNCTIONS OF @MARVEL EXCEPT AAH
)@@G@@LPHABETIZING.  THE S,   @G@@@@R, AND A OPTIONS CAUSE SYMBOLIC, RELOCATABAI
)@@G@@LE, AND ABSOLUTE ELEMENTS     @G@@@@TO BE PUNCHED, RESPECTIVELY.  WHEN TAJ
)@@G@@HE N OPTION IS PRESENT, RELOCATABLE @G@@@@AND ABSOLUTE ELEMENTS WILL BE AK

)@@G@@WHEN THE N OPTION IS NOT PRESENT, RELOCATABLE   @G@@@@AND ABSOLUTE ELEMEAM
)@@G@@NTS WILL BE PUNCHED FROM THE FILE IN WHICH @MARVEL    @F@@@@CAUSES THEM AN
)@@G@@TO BE PLACED (THE FILE NAMED IN SPEC2, OR IF SPEC2 IS @G@@@@ABSENT, THE AO
)@@G@@FILE NAMED IN SPEC1).  THE G, J, AND H OPTIONS AND SEQ-CHAR @C@@@@ARE ASAP
)@@G@@ DESCRIBED WITH THE FURPUR @PCH COMMAND.  @@@@@@@H@@@@@MARVEL CAN BE EXPAQ
)@@G@@ENSIVE TO USE AS IT CAUSES COMPILATIONS OF ALL ELEMENTS     @F@@@@TO BE AR
)@@G@@DONE.  IF A SIMPLE LISTING IS ALL THAT IS DESIRED, THE @SEND@B@@@@PROCESAS
)@@G@@SOR MAY BE USED FOR THIS PURPOSE.   @@@@@@@]@@@@EXAMPLES:   @@@@@@@^@@@@AT
)@@G@@ @MARVEL  TPF$.,TPF$.   @[@@@@ @EOF @@@@@@@F@@@@THE SYMBOLICS IN TPF$ ARAU

)@@G@@       CHKASG     @A@@@@      SUBROUTINE CHKASG ( IFN,$ )   @[@@@@C     BX
)@@G@@@B@@@@C  CHECK TOO INSURE IFN IS ASSIGNED S/R.  @[@@@@C     @ @@@@      BY
)@@G@@IMPLICIT INTEGER (A-Z)  @ @@@@      COMMON /FACPKT/FACPKT(9)@^@@@@      BZ
)@@G@@DIMENSION IFN(2)  @[@@@@C     @B@@@@      IF ( IFN(1).EQ.'      ' )RETURCA
)@@G@@N     @ @@@@      IF ( IFN(1).EQ.0 )RETURN@^@@@@      FACPKT(1)=IFN(1)  CB
)@@G@@@^@@@@      FACPKT(2)=IFN(2)  @B@@@@      CALL MOVER ( 0,0,FACPKT(3),1,7CC
)@@G@@ )    @E@@@@      CALL FACIL ( FACPKT)           @ GET FACILITY PACKET  CD
)@@G@@@E@@@@      IF ( FLD(0,6,FACPKT(7)).GT.0 )GO TO 11 @ IFN ASSIGNED?@E@@@@CE

)@@G@@ )    @D@@@@      IF ( STAT.LT.0 )GO TO 22        @ ASSIGN OK?    @C@@@@CI
)@@G@@   11 RETURN                          @ YES     @D@@@@   22 CALL OPA ( -CJ

)@@G@@@A@@@@      CALL OPA ( 40,'STATUS=&' )    @A@@@@      CALL OPOP ( 1,48,SCL
)@@G@@TAT,14 )    @#@@@@      RETURN 2    @]@@@@      END   @^@@@@-30,30      CM
)@@G@@ CHKASG     @[@@@@*IQUAL@#@@@@-1,25        IQUAL@B@@@@      SUBROUTINE ICN
)@@G@@QUAL ( IFN,BUF,CNT )    @[@@@@C     @^@@@@C     IMPLIED QUAL S/R  @C@@@@CO
)@@G@@C     ADJUST *FILE NAME IN BUF TO QUAL*FILE.    @[@@@@C     @ @@@@      CP

)@@G@@,1,BUF,K+1,CNT )  @ ADD '*FILE' (QUAL*FILE)     @#@@@@      CNT=CNT + K DA
)@@G@@@]@@@@      RETURN@]@@@@      END   @#@@@@-26,27       IQUAL___     MOVEDB
